<Date>1538865272734</Date><Text>This is the devil in disguise. I say that because you wouldn't typically see any red flags at first glance. However, the situation got so severe, we will be filing an official complaint with our insurance company. If you don't want to read all of this, just skip to #4 in Cons list.

Disclaimer: most of the positive reviews for this place are made by people with no Yelp history or profile picture. Looks like paid reviews for me.

Pros:
1. The place is clean and looks nice.
2. The equipment is new and up-to-date.
3. The dental assistant is nice.

Cons (from least problematic to downright atrocious):
1. They almost never pick up the phone. You have to make several attempts to make an appointment, and even more so to get test results or information. Oh, BTW, they don't call you with your x-ray results. You have to call THEM. What kind of dentist even does this?
2. The receptionist is not friendly. She looks annoyed every time you approach her with a question, and gives you very reluctant responses.
3. The time you scheduled your appointment for doesn't matter; expect to wait. During my last cleaning app, I had to wait for over an hour to be seen. Watching the doctor chat it up with the receptionist definitely didn't make things any better. When I was finally seen by Dr. Tsang, she didn't even apologize for making me wait or acknowledge my time in any way. She then spent LESS than 10 minutes cleaning my teeth. I have permanent retainers, and the cleaning should never be this fast. My plaque came back a few days later.
4. The treatment they offer is VERY bad. Dr. Tsang actually messed up my husband's cavity fillings. She didn't bond them to the to tooth and the cavity ended up popping out. All the cavities had holes in them, and my husband kept getting food stuck in them, which is very dangerous. The deep cleaning we paid $400 for was half-done and there were still a lot of things stuck underneath the gum. We have to re-do EVERYTHING. In addition, the process is EXTREMELY painful. Dr. Tsang is very cold and clearly doesn't care about making the process less painful in any way. My husband had to suffer all that pain for NOTHING.
5. They have absolutely NO MORALS. They don't just try to up-sell you on treatments you don't need or on more expensive treatments. They actually LIE to you and say your insurance DOESN'T cover the treatment you're seeking. Example #1: they told my husband they don't offer the cavity fillings that our insurance covers, and told him it would cost him $300 per cavity. My husband then called our insurance, and what do you know? OF COURSE they have the cavity fillings our insurance covers. We had to battle them for an hour before he could get the treatment he needed. Example #2: when I inquired about removing my permanent retainers, they said it would cost $400 to remove, and another $600 for the mouth guard (which, BTW, isn't even an official retainer) to wear at night. I looked it up; a mouth guard doesn't cost more than $100 on Amazon. They will try to pull a fast one on you at every turn, any time you need anything done. They are simply banking on the fact that you will trust them (since they are DOCTORS) and pay blindly. Absolute disgrace. I don't even want to think about all the people who fell for this trap.

Bottom line: I never write reviews unless I feel like I should really warn people about a shady business. This is most certainly one of them. Don't waste your precious time, money, nerves and teeth on this terrible place.<//Text><Response>None<//Response>< gmapID>

< Text>
Taco Bell next door? Hard pass. Looking for a better taste? El Faro. Grab a large Jamaica or a delicious Horchata with your dependable quesadillas. Feeling adventurous with the new trends? Go there on the weekend only for some birria tacos that are possibly their most delicious items. Feeling like a philly cheese steak that's improved or a memory of a state fair cheese steak sandwich? Grab the steak and cheese torta and don't look back!

From nachos to dinner plates and even a shrimp burrito, you can't go too wrong here. I'm not necessarily a fan of the steamed tortilla but they're happy to grill upon request. Nor am I'm usually thrilled about their guac because it's a little thin for my taste. But I GUARANTEE once you taste their salsa you'll be hooked. You'll never look back next door for any fire or diablo sauce. Come grab an extra salsa that's laced with a hint of habanero and thank me later.

Enjoy a meal made with consistency and don't be afraid to say hi inside.<//Text>

<UserId.>106571844991994537946<//UserId.>< review>
I used to love El Faro! It was my go to breakfast spot. They always had the best salsa and ingredients. That is until this last month. This last month has been a real hassle with all the pandemic related issues. (understandably) I have tried calling at least 30 different times and out of those times only been picked up 2 times. To make things worse I wasn't allowed to order two hours after they had opened because they said that they were not ready to take orders. When I was finally able to order after trying to order for 2 hours the only day that they decided to take my order, they took forever to make my food and I was the only customer there! It also made me feel really sad because it was not even close to how good it used to be. I say this with a heavy heavy heart but I don't think I will be returning anymore. Two years of going there every day and its such a shame that now they don't seem to care about the quality of their food or the service they provide to their customers.

< text>
Service
The ladies in the kitchen are like family and they put that love into the food and service. Really nice ladies.

The cashier wasn't very friendly but he gets the job done.

Food
The breakfast burritos are good. The portion size is just right and remember to ask for a little extra house salsa. Yum.

The lunch food is standard trattoria fare. It's a little salty but never leaves you hungry.

Location
The location is safe and easy to get to from Bart, bus and car.</text>

< Review>
This is one of the best 'classic' taquerias downtown. The prices are great, the food is very generously portioned and exactly what you'd expect from a taqueria.  El Faro has other locations and they are all delicious. There are other places that do the same thing within a few blocks, but no one makes the comfort-food level tastiness like El Faro. The Happy Burrito is the go-to with all the fixings. Also open for breakfast (best hangover breakfast burrito downtown.)<//Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
While somewhat pricey, the seats are lavish recliners with tons of space between seats and between rows. The concessions stand has a decent mix of traditional fare and some pleasing additions, like hot cinnamon roll bites and coffee. The theater itself is reasonably clean; parking is usually available just putside the front.</review>

<text>Came across this place during grocery shopping and I was pleasantly surprised.  The interior felt like a restaurant and not your regular fast food place.  Table and seats were high and there were also regular seating too.  After I ordered, I was given a number, which I took to my table.  I really liked seeing the sink by the counter, where I could just wash my hands before eating.  My burger was delivered to my table and all the condiments and napkins were at the table too. None of those little packets and napkin dispensers at the counter to mess about.  The burger was tasty and looked freshly made and all the onions and tomatoes freshly cut.  Worth a visit for a quick bite and friendly staff that keep the place clean and inviting.

I had eaten somewhat recently and wasnt overly hungry so I opted for just the single patty burger with no fries or drink but with all the toppings it was as big as a double or triple anyway and satisfying. The angus burger on special was topped with beef brisket, bacon, cheddar, and pickles and the huge stack of juicy, crisp, cheese covered meat was delicious. The pickles went well with the other salty flavors and the hearty bun had no issues handling the mountain of greasy meats. I didnt notice any of the bbq sauce I was expecting on it but they threw in a few packs of ketchup which I didnt use and it was great dry regardless.

Staff were friendly and service quick and efficient. They took every corona safety precaution I could think of with sanitizers, social distancing markers, and staff decked out in protective gear. No outdoor dining area and just carryout and delivery orders currently tho.<//text>< name>
Stops Susan<//name>

<GmapID>0x808f7e2fcae1b335:0xe188bf359e46ad52< /GmapID>< text>
This place is in the same class as Burger Joint and Super Duper.  A premium priced fast food of better quality.  The burgers range from 6-7$ alone, with small sides of fries for around $2.
I ordered a truffle swiss chicken sandwich with smash fries (super thin fries tossed in garlic, rosemary, olive oil).  The fries were a bit over oily and salty, but were crispy and tasty.  The thinness made them not ideal vehicles for ketchup.  The sandwich looked thrown together with the bun not even covering most of the chicken, and they forgot to put veggies in it I had to bring it back.  It was also really greasy but tasted good.  I ended up with a strange stomach ache so I walked around Ross in the plaza which is extremely depressing.  Not likely to repeat here without coupon.< /text>

< review>
I think Smashburger is just splendid. For a small-ish chain (at least in terms of CA locations), they have solid burgers that taste fresh and and a good value. I really like some of their more healthy options like the chicken burgers on wheat. I can't wait to try their new burgers that have cucumbers, goat cheese and spinach on them as toppings. I personally like their Avocado Chicken Club, without mayo. They usually put a light amount of ranch on it, which I appreciate. Their chicken always comes out juicy, albeit, thin. Their sweet potato fries and smash fries are also good. I also like how they have Honest Tea brewing. I always stop by when I'm in the area running errands.</review>

<Review>This was my second visit to this location. Both were bad experiences. After waiting for 25 minutes, I never actually got my burger. They put all of their focus on DoorDash orders at the sacrifice of all sit-down customers (about 10 people). You place an order at the counter and then sit at a table with your order number. 5 out of the 10 people waiting at tables had their order "lost".

This place wants to have a gimmick and be something like Five Guys but it can't even compete with a quality burger from Jack-In-The-Box.

Both times, my order was taken by a careless staff member. I was never explained what the "smash" process was and was not asked for a temp on my meat. (For my first visit) what I got was an expensive and very mediocre greasy thin burger on what seems like a store bought bun. Not worth it.

Atmosphere is a step up from fast food environment. Save your money for a Five Guys Burger or Jack-In-The-Box. Both deliver better products and experience.< /Review>< Rate>

< Date>
1465169507549</Date>
< rating>
3</rating>
<Text>I came here for an event a few weeks back, and basically got to try, well, every single one of the items on their menu, so I'm not going to go and rate each individual one. But, overall, everything they have to offer is pretty solid, from their various burgers, to their sides, to their shakes (which are made with Haagen Daz ice cream!). Fantastic, they are not, but solid, they are, falling somewhere in between the fast food world and the fancy burger world, in the same tier as, say, Super Duper.

Some interesting tidbits: they're named what they are because they take fresh meat (ground beef, chicken, etc) and smash it into a super hot griddle, which simultaneously sears, steams, and quickly cooks the meat. Also, while they have set items on their menus, their burgers are actually customizable, for those who like playing with their food. And with the variety of buns, proteins, and ingredients to pick from, there's plenty of combinations to come up with!

***Accessibility Info***

Venue - Spacious venue, with a combination of inaccessible counter height tables, and lower standard height tables and booths.

Bathroom - Didn't check them out, but I imagine they're okay.<//Text><pictures>None</pictures>< resp>
None< /resp>
